## Summary

**Fix Applied:**

Added `#include <lustre_compat/linux/linux-misc.h>` to `include/lustre_compat/linux/linux-fs.h` at line 27.

**Rationale:**

The compile error occurred due to an **include order dependency issue**:

1. The file `linux-fs.h` uses the function `user_backed_iter()` in the `iov_iter_get_pages_alloc2()` function (line 269)
2. However, `user_backed_iter()` is defined in `linux-misc.h` (line 48)
3. When `mdt_fs.c` included `linux-fs.h` before `linux-misc.h` was transitively included, the compiler encountered the use of `user_backed_iter()` before its declaration, causing an implicit declaration
4. Later, when `linux-misc.h` was included (via `mdt_internal.h`), the compiler found a conflicting explicit definition

**The fix ensures that `linux-misc.h` is included in `linux-fs.h` before `user_backed_iter()` is used**, resolving the declaration order conflict. This is a standard C programming practice where header files must include their dependencies to be self-contained.


Request ID: de0342c0-687e-4c40-891a-129c1f74de91
